## 1. Overview

The **Arguments Tab** is the central hub for argumentation within a deliberation. It provides a comprehensive interface for:

- **Viewing** all structured arguments in AIF (Argument Interchange Format)
- **Creating** new arguments using argumentation schemes
- **Analyzing** argument schemes and multi-scheme networks
- **Evaluating** arguments through ASPIC+ formal theory
- **Attacking** arguments strategically using critical questions

### Key Frameworks Integrated

| Framework | Purpose | Implementation |
|-----------|---------|----------------|
| **AIF** | Argument Interchange Format for semantic representation | JSON-LD export, node/edge modeling |
| **ASPIC+** | Structured argumentation with defeasible reasoning | Theory evaluation, extensions, rationality checks |
| **Walton Schemes** | Argumentation scheme taxonomy | 60+ schemes with critical questions |
| **Multi-Scheme Nets** | Complex argument structures | Serial, convergent, divergent, hybrid patterns |

### Design Philosophy

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
```

### Tab Configuration

| Tab Value | Label | Icon | Component |
|-----------|-------|------|-----------|
| `list` | All Arguments | `List` | `AIFArgumentsListPro` |
| `create` | Create Argument | `PlusCircle` | `AIFArgumentWithSchemeComposer` |
| `schemes` | Schemes | `Network` | `SchemesSection` |
| `networks` | Networks | `GitFork` | `NetworksSection` |
| `create-net` | Create Argument Net | `Workflow` | `NetsTab` |
| `aspic` | ASPIC | `Shield` | `AspicTheoryPanel` + `ConflictResolutionPanel` |

## 4. Component Props & State

### Props Interface

```typescript
interface ArgumentsTabProps {
  // Core identifiers
  deliberationId: string;          // Current deliberation context
  authorId: string;                // User creating/viewing arguments
  
  // UI Control
  refreshCounter: number;          // Triggers list refresh
  dsMode?: boolean;                // Dialogue System mode (affects UI)
  
  // Callbacks
  onArgumentClick?: (argument: any) => void;
  onViewDialogueMove?: (moveId: string, delibId: string) => void;
  onVisibleTextsChanged?: (texts: string[]) => void;
  onTabChange?: (tab: DeliberationTab) => void;
  setHighlightedDialogueMoveId?: (id: string | null) => void;
}
```

### Internal State

```typescript
// User identification (fetched on mount)
const [currentUserId, setCurrentUserId] = useState<string | null>(null);

// ArgumentNetAnalyzer dialog state
const [netAnalyzerOpen, setNetAnalyzerOpen] = useState(false);
const [selectedArgumentId, setSelectedArgumentId] = useState<string | null>(null);

// Attack generation dialog state
const [attackTargetId, setAttackTargetId] = useState<string | null>(null);
const [attackTargetClaimId, setAttackTargetClaimId] = useState<string | null>(null);
const [selectedAttack, setSelectedAttack] = useState<AttackSuggestion | null>(null);
const [wizardOpen, setWizardOpen] = useState(false);

// Refresh mechanism
const [attackRefreshKey, setAttackRefreshKey] = useState(0);
```

## 5. Sub-Tab: All Arguments (List)

### Component: `AIFArgumentsListPro`

**Location:** `components/arguments/AIFArgumentsListPro.tsx`  
**Size:** ~1,442 lines  
**Purpose:** Display all arguments in a deliberation with rich metadata and interactions

### Architecture


### Data Fetching Strategy

```typescript
// Primary: Paginated argument list with SWR Infinite
useSWRInfinite(
  (pageIndex, previousPageData) => {
    if (previousPageData && !previousPageData.hasMore) return null;
    return `/api/arguments?deliberationId=${deliberationId}&page=${pageIndex}&limit=40`;
  },
  fetcher
);

// Secondary: Batch AIF metadata (eliminates N+1)
GET /api/arguments/aif/batch?ids=arg1,arg2,arg3...

// Tertiary: Evidential confidence scores
useEvidentialConfidence(argumentIds, deliberationId);

// Reference: Scheme definitions
fetchSchemes() // from @/lib/client/aifApi
```

### AIF Metadata Structure

```typescript
type AifMeta = {
  scheme?: { 
    id: string; 
    key: string; 
    name: string; 
    slotHints?: Record<string, string>;
  } | null;
  
  schemes?: Array<{  // Multi-scheme support
    id: string;
    key: string;
    name: string;
    role: "PRIMARY" | "SUPPORTING" | "DERIVED";
    isPrimary: boolean;
    confidence: number;
    explicitness: "EXPLICIT" | "IMPLICIT" | "INFERRED";
  }>;
  
  conclusion?: { id: string; text: string } | null;
  premises?: Array<{ id: string; text: string }> | null;
  implicitWarrant?: { text: string } | null;
  
  attacks?: {
    REBUTS: number;     // Attacks on conclusion
    UNDERCUTS: number;  // Attacks on inference
    UNDERMINES: number; // Attacks on premises
  } | null;
  
  cq?: {
    required: number;   // Total CQs for scheme
    satisfied: number;  // CQs addressed
  };
  
  preferences?: {
    preferredBy: number;
    dispreferredBy: number;
  };
  
  provenance?: {
    kind: "ORIGINAL" | "IMPORTED" | "GENERATED";
    sourceDeliberationId?: string;
    sourceDeliberationName?: string;
    fingerprint?: string;
  } | null;
};
```

### Key Callbacks

```typescript
// Opens ArgumentNetAnalyzer for multi-scheme analysis
onAnalyzeArgument={(argId) => {
  setSelectedArgumentId(argId);
  setNetAnalyzerOpen(true);
}}

// Opens attack generation flow
onGenerateAttack={(argId, claimId) => {
  setAttackTargetId(argId);
  setAttackTargetClaimId(claimId);
}}

// Navigate to dialogue move origin
onViewDialogueMove={(moveId, delibId) => {
  setHighlightedDialogueMoveId?.(moveId);
  onTabChange?.("dialogue");
}}
```

## 6. Sub-Tab: Create Argument

### Component: `AIFArgumentWithSchemeComposer`

**Location:** `components/arguments/AIFArgumentWithSchemeComposer.tsx`  
**Size:** ~1,592 lines  
**Purpose:** Create new arguments using argumentation schemes with full AIF/ASPIC+ integration

### Props Interface

```typescript
interface AIFArgumentWithSchemeComposerProps {
  deliberationId: string;
  authorId: string;
  
  // Pre-populated conclusion (optional)
  conclusionClaim: { id?: string; text?: string } | null;
  
  // Pre-selected scheme
  defaultSchemeKey?: string | null;
  
  // Attack context for creating attacks
  attackContext?: AttackContext | null;
  
  // Callbacks
  onCreated?: (argumentId: string) => void;
  onCreatedDetail?: (arg: { id: string; conclusion: any; premises: any[] }) => void;
  onChangeConclusion?: (c: { id?: string; text?: string } | null) => void;
}

interface AttackContext {
  mode: "REBUTS" | "UNDERCUTS" | "UNDERMINES";
  targetArgumentId?: string;
  targetClaimId?: string;
  targetPremiseId?: string;
}
```

### State Management

```typescript
// Scheme selection
const [schemes, setSchemes] = useState<ArgumentScheme[]>([]);
const [selectedSchemeKey, setSelectedSchemeKey] = useState<string | null>(null);

// Argument structure
const [premises, setPremises] = useState<PremiseInput[]>([]);
const [majorPremise, setMajorPremise] = useState<string>("");
const [minorPremise, setMinorPremise] = useState<string>("");
const [conclusion, setConclusion] = useState<{ id?: string; text?: string } | null>(null);

// ASPIC+ configuration
const [ruleType, setRuleType] = useState<"STRICT" | "DEFEASIBLE">("DEFEASIBLE");
const [premisesAreAxioms, setPremisesAreAxioms] = useState(false);

// Evidence
const [pendingCitations, setPendingCitations] = useState<Citation[]>([]);

// UI state
const [contradictionModal, setContradictionModal] = useState<ContradictionInfo | null>(null);
const [isSubmitting, setIsSubmitting] = useState(false);
```

### Attack Context Integration

When creating an argument as an attack, the composer automatically creates a `ConflictApplication`:

```typescript
// Attack Type: REBUTS (attacks conclusion)
if (attackContext.mode === "REBUTS") {
  await postCA({
    conflictingClaimId: newConclusionId,    // The attack claim
    conflictedClaimId: attackContext.targetClaimId,  // Target conclusion
    type: "REBUTS",
    deliberationId,
    authorId,
  });
}

// Attack Type: UNDERCUTS (attacks inference)
if (attackContext.mode === "UNDERCUTS") {
  await postCA({
    conflictingClaimId: newConclusionId,
    conflictedArgumentId: attackContext.targetArgumentId,  // Target argument
    type: "UNDERCUTS",
    deliberationId,
    authorId,
  });
}

// Attack Type: UNDERMINES (attacks premise)
if (attackContext.mode === "UNDERMINES") {
  await postCA({
    conflictingClaimId: newConclusionId,
    conflictedClaimId: attackContext.targetPremiseId,  // Target premise
    type: "UNDERMINES",
    deliberationId,
    authorId,
  });
}
```

## 7. Sub-Tab: Schemes

### Component: `SchemesSection`

**Location:** `components/deepdive/v3/sections/SchemesSection.tsx`  
**Size:** ~298 lines  
**Purpose:** Display detected argumentation schemes grouped by type

### SchemeCard Component

```typescript
interface SchemeGroup {
  schemeKey: string;
  schemeName: string;
  arguments: ArgumentInfo[];
  averageConfidence: number;
}

// Rendered for each detected scheme
<SchemeCard
  schemeKey={group.schemeKey}
  schemeName={group.schemeName}
  argumentCount={group.arguments.length}
  avgConfidence={group.averageConfidence}
  arguments={group.arguments}
  onArgumentClick={handleArgumentClick}
/>
```

## 8. Sub-Tab: Networks

### Component: `NetworksSection`

**Location:** `components/deepdive/v3/sections/NetworksSection.tsx`  
**Size:** ~342 lines  
**Purpose:** Detect and display multi-scheme argument networks (nets)

### NetCandidate Data Structure

```typescript
interface NetCandidate {
  id: string;
  rootArgumentId: string;
  netType: "convergent" | "linked" | "serial" | "divergent" | "hybrid";
  complexity: number;     // Number of steps/arguments
  confidence: number;     // Overall confidence (0-1)
  
  schemes: Array<{
    schemeId: string;
    schemeName: string;
    schemeCategory: string;
    role: "ROOT" | "SUPPORTING" | "LINKING";
  }>;
  
  relationships: Array<{
    sourceScheme: string;
    targetScheme: string;
    type: "SUPPORTS" | "REQUIRES" | "CHAINS_TO";
  }>;
}
```

## 9. Sub-Tab: Create Argument Net

### Component: `NetsTab`

**Size:** ~400 lines  
**Purpose:** Full management interface for argument nets

### Net Data Structure

```typescript
interface Net {
  id: string;
  argumentId: string;
  argumentConclusion: string;
  netType: "serial" | "convergent" | "divergent" | "hybrid";
  overallConfidence: number;
  stepCount: number;
  
  steps: Array<{
    id: string;
    order: number;
    schemeId: string;
    schemeName: string;
    label: string;
    confidence: number;
    inputFromStep: number | null;  // For serial chains
  }>;
  
  weakestStep: {
    id: string;
    stepOrder: number;
    confidence: number;
    label: string;
  };
  
  author: {
    id: string;
    username: string;
    name: string;
    image: string | null;
  };
}
```

## 10. Sub-Tab: ASPIC

### Components: `AspicTheoryPanel` + `ConflictResolutionPanel`

The ASPIC tab integrates two main components for formal argumentation theory evaluation.

### AspicTheoryPanel

**Location:** `components/aspic/AspicTheoryPanel.tsx`  
**Purpose:** Display ASPIC+ theory evaluation with formal semantics

### ASPIC+ Theory Structure

```typescript
interface AspicTheory {
  // Knowledge Base
  K: {
    axioms: string[];        // Kâ‚: cannot be attacked
    ordinary: string[];      // Kâ‚’: can be undermined
  };
  
  // Rules
  R: {
    strict: AspicRule[];     // Râ‚›: cannot be undercut
    defeasible: AspicRule[]; // Ráµˆ: can be undercut
  };
  
  // Contraries function
  contraries: Map<string, string[]>;
  
  // Preference ordering
  preferences: AspicPreference[];
}

interface AspicRule {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  antecedent: string[];
  consequent: string;
  type: "STRICT" | "DEFEASIBLE";
}

interface AspicPreference {
  preferredId: string;
  dispreferredId: string;
  basis: "SPECIFICITY" | "AUTHORITY" | "RECENCY" | "EXPLICIT";
  strength: number;
}
```

### Resolution Strategy Types

```typescript
type ResolutionStrategy = 
  | "remove_weakest"    // Remove preference with lowest confidence
  | "remove_oldest"     // Keep most recent preferences
  | "vote_based"        // Remove minority opinion preference
  | "user_selection";   // Manual selection

interface ConflictResolution {
  cycleId: string;
  strategy: ResolutionStrategy;
  removedPreferenceId: string;
  justification: string;
}
```

---

The Arguments Tab includes a sophisticated attack generation system with three modal dialogs.

### AttackSuggestion Data Structure

```typescript
interface AttackSuggestion {
  id: string;
  type: "REBUTS" | "UNDERCUTS" | "UNDERMINES";
  
  // Attack content
  suggestedText: string;
  rationale: string;
  
  // Strategic metrics (0-10)
  strategicValue: number;  // Overall effectiveness
  strength: number;        // Argument strength
  difficulty: number;      // Ease of construction
  burden: number;          // Evidence burden
  
  // Critical questions exploited
  criticalQuestions: Array<{
    cqId: string;
    cqText: string;
    exploitStrategy: string;
  }>;
  
  // Target info
  targetPremiseId?: string;  // For UNDERMINES
  targetRuleId?: string;     // For UNDERCUTS
}
```

### AttackArgumentWizard Component

**Location:** `components/argumentation/AttackArgumentWizard.tsx`  
**Size:** ~959 lines

## 12. API Routes Reference

### Arguments API

| Route | Method | Purpose | Request Body | Response |
|-------|--------|---------|--------------|----------|
| `/api/arguments` | GET | List arguments | Query: `deliberationId`, `page`, `limit`, `schemeKey`, `q` | `{ arguments: ArgumentInfo[], hasMore: boolean }` |
| `/api/arguments` | POST | Create argument | `{ deliberationId, authorId, conclusionId, premiseIds, schemeId, ruleType }` | `{ id, conclusion, premises, scheme }` |
| `/api/arguments/aif/[id]` | GET | Get AIF metadata | - | `AifMeta` |
| `/api/arguments/aif/batch` | GET | Batch AIF metadata | Query: `ids` (comma-separated) | `Record<string, AifMeta>` |
| `/api/arguments/cq/[id]` | GET | Get critical questions | - | `{ required: CQ[], satisfied: CQ[] }` |
| `/api/arguments/attacks/generate` | POST | Generate attack suggestions | `{ targetClaimId, targetArgumentId, userId }` | `AttackSuggestion[]` |
| `/api/arguments/export` | POST | Export as AIF JSON-LD | `{ deliberationId }` | AIF JSON-LD document |

### Claims API

| Route | Method | Purpose | Request Body | Response |
|-------|--------|---------|--------------|----------|
| `/api/claims` | POST | Create claim | `{ text, deliberationId, authorId }` | `{ id, text }` |
| `/api/claims/[id]/citations` | POST | Add citation | `{ citationId }` | `{ success: true }` |

### Conflict Applications API

| Route | Method | Purpose | Request Body | Response |
|-------|--------|---------|--------------|----------|
| `/api/ca` | POST | Create conflict | `{ conflictingClaimId, conflictedClaimId/ArgumentId, type, deliberationId, authorId }` | `{ id, type }` |

### ASPIC API

| Route | Method | Purpose | Request Body | Response |
|-------|--------|---------|--------------|----------|
| `/api/aspic/evaluate` | POST | Evaluate theory | `{ deliberationId }` | `AspicEvaluation` |
| `/api/aspic/conflicts` | GET | Get preference conflicts | Query: `deliberationId` | `ConflictCycle[]` |
| `/api/aspic/resolve` | POST | Resolve conflict | `{ cycleId, strategy, removedPreferenceId }` | `{ success: true }` |

### Nets API

| Route | Method | Purpose | Request Body | Response |
|-------|--------|---------|--------------|----------|
| `/api/nets` | GET | List nets | Query: `deliberationId` | `Net[]` |
| `/api/nets` | POST | Create net | `{ argumentId, netType, steps }` | `Net` |
| `/api/nets/detect` | POST | Detect nets | `{ argumentId, deliberationId }` | `NetCandidate[]` |
| `/api/nets/[id]` | GET | Get net details | - | `Net` |
| `/api/nets/[id]/confirm` | POST | Confirm detected net | - | `Net` |
| `/api/nets/[id]/cqs` | GET | Get composed CQs | - | `ComposedCQ[]` |

### Schemes API

| Route | Method | Purpose | Request Body | Response |
|-------|--------|---------|--------------|----------|
| `/api/schemes` | GET | List all schemes | - | `ArgumentScheme[]` |
| `/api/schemes/[key]` | GET | Get scheme details | - | `ArgumentScheme` |

---

### 13.2 Attack Generation Flow


---

## 16. Summary

The Arguments Tab in DeepDivePanelV2 provides a comprehensive argumentation management system built on three theoretical foundations:

1. **AIF (Argument Interchange Format)**: Semantic representation and export
2. **ASPIC+**: Formal structured argumentation with defeasible reasoning
3. **Walton Schemes**: Argumentation scheme taxonomy with critical questions

### Key Features

| Feature | Component | Purpose |
|---------|-----------|---------|
| Argument List | `AIFArgumentsListPro` | View all arguments with metadata |
| Argument Creation | `AIFArgumentWithSchemeComposer` | Create scheme-based arguments |
| Scheme Analysis | `SchemesSection` | Group arguments by scheme |
| Network Detection | `NetworksSection` | Find multi-scheme patterns |
| Net Management | `NetsTab` | Create and manage argument nets |
| ASPIC Evaluation | `AspicTheoryPanel` | Formal theory evaluation |
| Conflict Resolution | `ConflictResolutionPanel` | Resolve preference cycles |
| Attack Generation | `AttackSuggestions` + `AttackArgumentWizard` | Strategic attack creation |
| Net Analysis | `ArgumentNetAnalyzer` | Analyze multi-scheme structures |

### Development Timeline

- **Week 5**: ArgumentNetAnalyzer integration for multi-scheme net analysis
- **Week 6**: AttackArgumentWizard integration for CQ-based attacks

---
